[100m  [97m- Medium parcel: all dimensions < 50cm, cost $8[39m                                                                                                                                                                     [49m
[100m  [97m- Large parcel: all dimensions < 100cm, cost $15[39m                                                                                                                                                                    [49m
[100m  [97m- XL parcel: any dimension >= 100cm, cost $25[39m                                                                                                                                                                       [49m
[100m                                                                                                                                                                                                                      [49m
[100m  [97mStep 1 assumptions:[39m                                                                                                                                                                                                 [49m
[100m  [97m- The library accepts an order containing one or more parcels.[39m                                                                                                                                                      [49m
[100m  [97m- Each parcel has a list of dimensions represented as positive numbers.[39m                                                                                                                                             [49m
[100m  [97m- Dimensions are provided in centimetres.[39m                                                                                                                                                                           [49m
[100m  [97m- The implementation should not assume fixed dimension names like length, width, and height.[39m                                                                                                                        [49m
[100m  [97m- At least one dimension is required per parcel.[39m                                                                                                                                                                    [49m
[100m  [97m- Boundary values move into the next category:[39m                                                                                                                                                                      [49m
[100m  [97m- 10cm is medium[39m                                                                                                                                                                                                    [49m
[100m  [97m- 50cm is large[39m                                                                                                                                                                                                     [49m
[100m  [97m- 100cm is XL[39m                                                                                                                                                                                                       [49m
[100m  [97m- Invalid input should throw a clear validation error.[39m                                                                                                                                                              [49m
[100m                                                                                                                                                                                                                      [49m
[100m  [97mTasks:[39m                                                                                                                                                                                                              [49m
[100m  [97m1. Define clear TypeScript types for:[39m                                                                                                                                                                               [49m

[100m  [97m- parcel type[39m                                                                                                                                                                                                       [49m

[100m  [97m- order pricing result[39m                                                                                                                                                                                              [49m
[100m  [97m2. Implement Step 1 pricing logic.[39m                                                                                                                                                                                  [49m
[100m  [97m3. Add Jest tests covering green paths:[39m                                                                                                                                                                             [49m
[100m  [97m- small parcel[39m                                                                                                                                                                                                      [49m
[100m  [97m- medium parcel[39m                                                                                                                                                                                                     [49m
[100m  [97m- large parcel[39m                                                                                                                                                                                                      [49m

[100m  [97m- multiple parcels in one order[39m                                                                                                                                                                                     [49m
[100m  [97m- total order cost[39m                                                                                                                                                                                                  [49m
